  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_114185d9-bcb2-4ffb-a312-7342920b62b3'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText17611664185176171296" style="display:none"><b>Vengeance will be hers.</b><br /><br /><b>Allison Sekemoto once struggled with the question: human or monster? With the death of her love, Zeke, she has her answer.</b><br /><br /><b>Monster.</b><br /><br />Allie will embrace her cold vampire side to hunt down and end Sarren, the psychopathic vampire who murdered Zeke. But the trail is bloody and long, and Sarren has left many surprises for Allie and her companions - her creator Kanin, and her blood brother, Jackal. The trail is leading straight to the one place they must protect at any cost - the last vampire-free zone on Earth, Eden. And Sarren has one final, brutal shock in store for Allie. <br /><br />In a ruined world where no life is sacred and former allies can turn on you in one heartbeat, Allie will face her darkest days. And if she succeeds, her triumph will be short-lived in the face of surviving forever alone.<br /><br />THE FINAL HUNT IS ON.</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=on-the-run">on-the-run</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=siblings">siblings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer698482973" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1220360643446409804">**Spoilers for book 2, minor spoilers for book 3**<blockquote>
  <i>“Say you love me, vampire girl,” he whispered, his voice low and husky. “Tell me...that this is forever.”<br/>“I love you,” I said immediately. “And if we have forever, there’s no one else I want to spend it with.”</i>
</blockquote><b>That sad, sad moment when your favorite YA vampire series turns into a soap opera.</b><br/><br/>This book broke my heart in a way that hasn't happened since Ginny x Harry. I absolutely loved the previous books in this series, despite the main characte</span>
  <span id="freeText1220360643446409804" style="display:none">**Spoilers for book 2, minor spoilers for book 3**<blockquote>
  <i>“Say you love me, vampire girl,” he whispered, his voice low and husky. “Tell me...that this is forever.”<br>“I love you,” I said immediately. “And if we have forever, there’s no one else I want to spend it with.”</i>
</blockquote><b>That sad, sad moment when your favorite YA vampire series turns into a soap opera.</b><br><br>This book broke my heart in a way that hasn't happened since Ginny x Harry. I absolutely loved the previous books in this series, despite the main character's (Allie) tendency to be <b>extremely emo and Harry-Potter-Order-of-the-Phoenix angsty</b>. In previous books, I made excuses for her emotions, her feels, her constant need to hang onto her humanity in the face of her darker nature of the vampiric beast within in the hopes that she will eventually mature and embrace her darkness. I gave Allie credit for her weakness throughout this series, in the hopes that finally she will grow the fuck up and get her priorities straight.<br><br>It didn't happen. Quite the opposite.<br><br><b>Allie is more whiny than ever. Zeke is an emo pussy beyond redemption.</b> The only saving grace to this book was the glorious motherfucker that is Jackal (LET ME LOVE YOU). Let me tell you how much I love Jackal. I don't just love him. I want to marry him. I want to grovel at his feet. I want to get down on my knees and worship him. I want to get down on my knees, and, well, let's not go into explicit details, now. ANYWAY. *ahem*<br><br>I alternated between pain and pleasure in this book. Pain because of Allie. Pleasure whenever Jackal opened his mouth to rip Allie a new one.<br><br><b>What hurts about this book is that Kagawa KNEW that Allie and Zeke are weak characters.</b> She deliberately wrote her that way, because everything Jackal said about Allie rings so true. Jackal is Allie's biggest critic, and he absolutely confronted Allie on all her emotional lovey dovey bullshit.<blockquote>
  <i>“Puppy, I am getting so tired of listening to you whine about this,” he snarled at Zeke. “This isn’t rocket science. If you don’t want to be a monster, don’t be a bloody monster! Be an uptight stick in the mud like Kanin. Be a self-righteous bleeding heart like Allison. Or you can stop agonizing about it and be a fucking monster."</i>
</blockquote>See? Jackal represented the POV that I feel a lot of readers can understand. Kagawa made Allie to be a weak character, an unreasonable one, a stubborn one, and <b>while I respect her choice as the writer to create her character in this way, I cannot love Allie knowing her incredible faults.</b><br><br><u>The Plot</u>: Zeke is dead. Or he's supposed to be. Allie is trying not to think about him. Allie, Jackal, and Kanin are on their way through the devastation that is the US trying to track down the brilliant genius, Sarren, who seeks to kill every living and undead creature left in the world.<br><br>Here's essentially how the book goes:<br><br>Allie: I WILL NOT THINK ABOUT ZEKE *breaks down into tears 5 minutes later* I WILL BE A BIG BAD ASS KILLER AND AVENGE MY LOVER'S DEATH. *breaks down again*<br>Jackal: LOL YOU ARE SO DUMB, FACE YOUR NATURE. BE LIKE ME! RAAAAWR!<br>Allie: SHUT UP. You are SUCH a jerk.<br>Jackal: And you want rainbows and unicorns and flowers, face the fucking truth.<br>Kanin: Children, stop that. We are trying to save the world.<br>Jackal: NEENER NEENER NEENER. Omg stop crying. Want some cheese to go with your whine, sister?<br>Allie: I swear to god if I hear another word out of you, I will take your balls and shove them so far up your anal sphinc...<br>Kanin: CHILDREN, PLEASE. We're under attack by an army of rabids!<br>Jackal and Allie: *DIIIIIIIIIIIIIE RABIDS*<br>Kanin: The most important thing to do now is to be smart. Stay together...<br>Allie: Ok, daddy. OOH, SARREN! *runs away*<br>Kanin: *facepalms*<br>Allie: OMG ZEKE. I THOUGHT YOU WERE DEAD.<br>Zeke: &lt;3<br>Allie: THIS IS TOO GOOD TO BE TRUE BUT WHO CARES &lt;333333<br>Zeke: *stabs Allie*<br>Allie: ?_? D:<br>Zeke: &gt;:D DIE BITCH! SARREN TURNED ME AND I WILL KILL YOU!!!!!!!!!! I AM EVIL NOW! I WILL SING THE EVIL SONG! I HAVE NO IDEA WHAT THAT MEANS!<br>Allie: ;_; But I love you. I WILL KILL YOU. OR KISS YOU. The words are right next to each other on the keyboard.<br>Zeke: I AM SAVED BY YOUR LOVE.<br>Kanin: What the heck? ?_?<br>Jackal: You can't be fucking serious<br>Allie: &lt;3<br>Zeke: &lt;3<br>Kanin: That's pretty cute, kids. I'm so happy that you're back together, but really, we're trying to find Sarren here, can we focus on the mission?<br>Jackal: For fuck's sakes, get your fucking priorities straight.<br>Allie: &lt;3 u Zeke!<br>Zeke: ;_; I'm a demon now. I'M A MONSTER. I HATE MYSELF.<br>Allie: &lt;333333 I DON'T CARE. YOU'RE MY ZEEEEEEEEEKE &lt;33333 You will always be good and wonderful despite the fact that you have a blood bond with the evil vampire master Sarren! I hope. And if I hope for something hard enough, it must be true!!!!11!111<br>Kanin: We're trying to save the world here. Children?<br>Jackal: GET THE FUCK OVER YOURSELF, ZEKE AND ALLIE. WE'RE IN THE MIDDLE OF A FUCKING BATTLE. THERE ARE CORPSES ALL OVER THE FUCKING PLACE.<br>Allie: Blood is red, and red is the official color of Valentine's Day, so it just makes the situation more romantic, you asshole. Go away so Zeke and I can love each other.<br>Kanin: Children? Children? Are you even listening to me?<br>Zeke: I'm evil ;_;<br>Allie: No, you're not, honeypie baby booboo<br>Zeke: I'm evil ;_;<br>Allie: No, you're not, sugarpunkins<br>Zeke: I'm evil ;_;<br>Allie: No, you're not, sweetsugarlips<br>Zeke: Kill me.<br>Allie: I'll kiss you instead, does that work?<br>Zeke: Yes :D But I'm evil ;_;<br>Jackal: ...<br>Kanin: I molest bunnies. I kill kittens. An UFO has abducted me. IS ANYONE LISTENING TO ME ANYMORE?<br>Allie and Zeke: *stares into each other's eyes* Yes, daddy.<br>Jackal: *STABBY STABBY STABBY*<br>Kanin: Ok, the important thing is to stay together. No heroics. We do this as a team.<br>Allie: *sees Sarren* DIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIIEEEEE MOTHERFUCKER<br>Kanin: Why do I even bother?<br><br>Meanwhile:<br>Sarren: MWAHAHAHAHA. I will destroy the world. I WILL KILL EVERYONE!<br>Sarren: After I make this long-ass speech about how much they suck compared to my evil genius.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397793926ra/9329080.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Allie</u>: <blockquote>
  <i>“Two lives for the rest of the world?” he continued. “Are you willing to sacrifice everything to save one and destroy another?”</i>
</blockquote><b>Allie needs to get her fucking priorities straight.</b> I remained angry at Allie throughout the book because she was such an immature, madly romantic, wildly emotional and angsty character. She has her eyes on the prize: the prize being Zeke. The rest of the world? <b>The fate of the world? Fuck them. All she cares about is Zeke.</b><br><br>Let's focus on one scene specifically. Allie has found out that Zeke has been turned by Sarren into a vampire. Zeke is now evil, he retains little memories of her. Allie wants to go back for Zeke. It is a bad decision to make, and Kanin wants to get the facts straight before Allie makes her choice.<blockquote>
  <i>“I want you to understand exactly what you are deciding, right now. If we return to the city for Jackal and Ezekiel, Sarren could reach Eden, complete whatever he is planning, and unleash a virus that could destroy everything. And if that happens, everything we’ve done here will be for nothing. Do you understand that?”</i>
</blockquote>It's pretty fucking clear. If Allie goes back, she risks endangering everything they've been fighting for. They are the last people who stand a chance at stopping Sarren. Without them, there is no hope. The fate of vampires and that of the surviving human rests on them. If they fail, the results are disastrous.<blockquote>
  <i>“I just want you to understand the potential consequences of tonight,” he went on. “If we are killed, if we cannot get to Sarren in time, everything could die. It will be like it was sixty years ago. You aren’t old enough to remember the days Before, but when Red Lung was at its peak, the entire world was madness and chaos. And when the rabids appeared, it became hell on earth.”</i>
</blockquote>Kanin makes it perfectly clear. It's up to them.<blockquote>
  <i>“It is...a very heavy weight to carry, Allison, the damnation of a world. I want you to be very certain, before we go any further. Is it worth it? Is he worth it?”</i>
</blockquote>And Allie's choice?<blockquote>
  <i>I already knew my answer. It was selfish, it was unreasonable, and I knew it was the wrong choice. But I looked up at Kanin, into his impassive face, and whispered, “Yes.”<br>“You are willing to let others die for this. To let Sarren win.”</i>
</blockquote><b>I am fucking DONE with Allie.</b><br><br><u>Zeke</u>: Excuse me while I get out the world's smallest violin for Zeke.<br><br><b>*Khanh starts playing while Zeke sings his song of emo*</b><blockquote>
  <i>“I’m a demon, and the sooner I take myself out of this world, the better.”<br><br>“I only have to understand one thing—I’m a demon. I may not have wanted it, but it’s what I am now.”<br><br>“This is what I am, Allison! I’m a demon—you know it as well as me.”<br><br>“I’m terrified that I won’t be able to fight this, that I’ll turn into a demon and lose my soul forever, if it’s not already gone."</i>
</blockquote><b>*While Zeke was crying, Khanh slowly switched her instrument to a cello. Khanh stops playing and bashes Zeke on the head with it*</b><br><br><u>Jackal</u>: I wanted to pump my fist in triumph every time Jackal spoke. His is the voice of destructive reason, and my god, I love him so much I could die. He gives it to Allie straight every time she's in one of her fluffy frilly lovey dovey self-pitying moods. When Allie and Zeke are having one of their Loving Moments in the middle of a fucking battlefield...<blockquote>
  <i>“Still incredible, vampire girl,” he whispered, sounding almost like himself again. “Dangerous, beautiful and unstoppable. You haven’t changed.”</i>
</blockquote>Jackal interrupts them to tell them to get their heads out of their asses and get back into the fucking moment.<blockquote>
  <i>“Oh, isn’t that sweet,” came Jackal’s loud, mocking voice before I could reply. “Let’s make goo-goo eyes at each other in the middle of a stinking corpse field, how very romantic.”</i>
</blockquote>I felt like Jackal was saying everything I was thinking. Every time Zeke or Allie have one of their nauseatingly self-pitying moments, Jackal is there to mock them to their face.<blockquote>
  <i>“Aw, isn’t that sweet.” And Jackal sauntered into view, smirk firmly in place. “But don’t wait around on my account. It’s not like I can’t wait for yet another riveting night of listening to you people whine at each other. Oh, woe is me, I’m a vampire. I’m a horrible monster who eats babies and murders bunnies, boo hoo hoo.”</i>
</blockquote>I would be ever so happy if Jackal had his own spinoff.</span>

  <span id="freeText9934354467468655743" style="display:none"><u>AFTER READING:</u> I need a hug. I need lots of hugs. I can't believe it's over now. The ending was beautiful and bittersweet. I cannot wait to fangirl with you all. <br><br>Allison, Zeke, Jackal, and Kanin... You will be missed. I cried so much. I will reread this series every time I'm sad, I swear. <br><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2014 April 9th</i>, <b> less than a week before the release!!</b> Who's excited?? I know I am!<br><br><blockquote>The door loomed dead ahead, and I didn't stop.  I didn't pause to reconsider my plan.  Whether I was walking into a trap or straight to my death.  Katana at my side, I strode up to the door and kicked it below the knob.  It flew open with a crash, nearly ripped off its hinges, and I stepped into the room.</blockquote><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2014 March 27</i>, <b>19 more days</b><br>Another teaser! To the people who have received an arc, no spoilers for the rest of us until the publication, please! <b>No matter how much and how loud we <i>beg.</i></b><br><blockquote>"Hey old man," Jackal called in a mocking voice, "you forgot to say 'if you kids don't stop I'm going to turn this car right around and then no one will go to Eden.'"</blockquote><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2014 March 19</i>, <b>27 days</b> before publication (less than a month!!!)<br><blockquote>I slumped in relief, then turned...to face a squadron of suspicious, hard-eyed soldiers, their assult rifles already trained on us all.</blockquote><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2014 March 6th</i> <b>Another teaser!</b><br><blockquote>I didn't answer, walking faster to get away from him, and he quickened his pace to keep up.<br><br>“Come on, sister, where’s that obnoxious morality you kept throwing in my face every two seconds? You’re making it very difficult to take any sort of pleasure in mocking it relentlessly.”</blockquote><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2014 March 1st</i>, 1 month and 15 days before publication <br><br>So, <b>they moved the publication date to April 15th!</b> Yaaaaay!! And HERE'S A SHORT TEASER FROM JULIE!<br><blockquote>Ignoring the pain, I snatched my katana from where it lay on the hood and roared a challenge to the giant bearing down on me.  As it loomed overhead, smashing down with a huge fist, I dodged aside, and its arm crunched into metal, leaving a deep hole behind.</blockquote><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2014 January 23, In the afternoon</i><br><br><b>A LITTLE TEASER NEVER HURT ANYONE</b> said no one ever <br><br>Scroll down for THE FOREVER SONG's first teaser:<br><blockquote>The smell of blood grew thicker once we were past the wall, though nothing moved on the narrow path that snaked between houses.  The flimsy wood and tin shanties were silent, dark, as we ventured deeper, passing snow covered porches and empty chairs.  Everything looked intact, undisturbed.  There were no bodies.  No corpses mutilated in their beds, no blood spattered over the walls of the few homes we ducked into.  There weren't even any dead animals in the tiny, trampled pasture past the main strip.  Just snow, and dark, and emptiness.    <br><br>            And yet, the smell of blood soaked this place, hanging thick on the air, making my stomach ache and the Hunger roar to life.  I bit it down, clenching my jaw to keep from snarling in frustration.  It had been too long.  I needed food. The scent of blood was driving me crazy, and the fact that there were no humans here made me furious.  Where were they?  It wasn't possible that an entire outpost of mortals would up and disappear without a trace.<br><br>            And then, as we followed the path around the pasture and up to the huge barn at the top of the rise, we found the townspeople.<br><br>            A massive, barren tree stood beside the barn, twisted branches clawing at the sky.  They creaked and swayed beneath the weight of dozens of bodies, hanging upside down from ropes tied to the limbs.  Men, women, even a few kids, swinging in the breeze, dangling arms stiff and white.  Their throats had been cut, and the base of the tree was stained black, the blood spilled and wasted in the snow.  But the smell nearly knocked me over regardless, and I clenched my fists, the Hunger raking my insides with fiery talons.        <br><br>            "Well," Jackal muttered, crossing his arms and gazing up at the tree, "isn't that festive."  His voice was tight, as if he too, was on the edge of losing it.  "I'm guessing this is the reason we haven't found a single bloodbag from here all the way back to New Covington."  He growled, shaking his head, lips curling back from his fangs. "This guy is really starting to piss me off."<br><br>            I swallowed the Hunger, trying to focus through the gnawing ache.  "Why James, don't tell me you feel sorry for the walking meatsacks," I taunted, because sometimes, goading Jackal was the only thing that kept my mind off everything else.  He snorted and rolled his eyes.<br><br>            "No, sister, I'm annoyed because they don't have the decency to be alive so I can eat them."</blockquote><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2014 January 23, Early morning</i><br><br>HOLY FUDGE BROWNIES THE COVER!!! I'm so done it's so beautiful and simple and it doesn't match the other covers but the birds flying omg kill me <br><br><b>I LOVE IT SO MUCH</b> <br><br>****************<br> <br><i>Updated: 2013 October 19</i><br><br>Dear Julie, <br><br>I'm not asking for "<b>and they lived happily ever after!</b>"<br><br>I'm just asking for "<b>AND THEY LIVED.</b>"<br><br>And by them I meant Kanin, Allie, <u>AND</u> Zeke.<br><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2013 September 25</i><br><br>You know what would be the best form of torture? <br><b>Making someone fall in love with a book that ends on a cliffhanger with a sequel that doesn't come out for a year.</b> <br><br>OH WAIT, THERE ARE PEOPLE WHO ALREADY DO THAT...they're called <i>authors.</i><br><br>JulieK is an expert.<br><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2013 September 22</i> <b>THE BLURB IS OUT!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i><b>VENGEANCE WILL BE HERS</b><br><br>Allison Sekemoto once struggled with the question: human or monster?<br><br>With the death of her love, Zeke, she has her answer.<br><br><b>MONSTER</b><br><br>Allie will embrace her cold vampire side to hunt down and end Sarren, the psychopathic vampire who murdered Zeke. But the trail is bloody and long, and Sarren has left many surprises for Allie and her companions—her creator, Kanin, and her blood brother, Jackal. The trail is leading straight to the one place they must protect at any cost—the last vampire-free zone on Earth, Eden. <b>And Sarren has one final, brutal shock in store for Allie.</b><br><br>In a ruined world where no life is sacred and former allies can turn on you in one heartbeat, Allie will face her darkest days. And if she succeeds, triumph is short-lived in the face of surviving forever alone.</i>
</blockquote><br>Holy Maria. Just shut up and take my money! ;_;<br><br>The feels is becoming too much. Like every month we get closer and closer to Spring 20-freaking-14 and then we get a blurb and soon a cover and my whole life is just shifting and it hurts so much because it said Zeke is dead aND JULIE KAGAWA WHY ARE YOU DOING THIS TO ME. <br><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2013 September 2</i> WE JUST GOT AN <b>EXPECTED PUBLICATION</b> PEOPLE!! *drum rolls*<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>April 29th 2014</b>
</blockquote><br><br>NO. But <b>that's a million light years away</b>?! <br><br><u>My feelings right now:</u><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/673049.gif" width="300" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/624531.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>THEN...</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421760i/838305.png" width="200" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>****************<br><br><i>Updated: 2013 August 19</i><br><br><b>THIS IS JUST TOO MUCH</b> *wails*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421760i/838306._SX540_.jpg" width="350" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****************<br><br><blockquote>And the monster rose up, embracing my pain, turning it to vengeance. <i><b>This is what we are</b></i>, it whispered, easing the despair threatening to crush me. <i><b>We are vampires. We are not human, we do not need human emotion, we do not get attached to human beings. You knew that from the beginning.</b></i><br><br>I did. Allie the Fringer knew that, even before she was Turned. She'd tried to warn me to keep my distance, to guard my heart. <br><br><b>Lesson learned. I was a monster. I would never forget that again.</b>
</blockquote><br>****************<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380421760ra/838307.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>My Dream Cast<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>YIFEI LIU</b> as Allison Sekemoto<br>"black hair, pale skin, and class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>or <b>Devon Aoki</b> for Allie<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>****************<br><br>Look at what you did to me, Julie. I'm infected. Slowly going mad and feverish. Perhaps I'm turning into a Bleeder? <br><br>Well, we all know there's only one cure for that. Four letters. It starts with a Z and ends with an E. Hurry, I need it fast. <br><br>****************<br><br>The Forever Song. I NEED THIS.<br><br>Omg. I haven't read The Eternity Cure but I'm sure it's amazing so I'm going to wait until July to read it coz I heard there's a cliffhanger and I don't wanna wait that long for this!<br><br>I said that all in one breath... in my mind.<br><br><b>Update 6/23:</b> Because I'm a stupid human being that lacks self-control, I foolishly went on and read <i>The Eternity Cure</i>. I tried not to do it. I truly did. But I am only human after all. Let's just say that there were a <i>lot</i> of screaming involved and more tissues that I can count on one hand were used.<br><br>Now, I TRULY NEED THIS. I am willing to give up my firstborn to get an arc. <s>READ THAT, JULIE? So if you ever want a baby, come find me in the next two weeks.</s><br><br><blockquote>
<b><i>You can't save anyone now. The requiem has started, and when the last melody plays, the only applause will be sweet, eternal silence.</i></b><br>-Sarren</blockquote></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_610231909" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/610231909" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/610231909?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer610231909" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9226554127713004566"><b>
  <i>"So, this is me, all of me, forever. No more looking back. No more regrets. From now on, vampire girl--" he lowered his head, brushing his lips across my skin "--I'm all yours."</i>
</b><br/><br/>I promise no spoilers for this book but it would be impossible to review <i>The Forever Song</i> without giving away some things from the previous books. In my opinion, <u>this final installment is the weakest</u>. I thought the second book was a hard one to follow, so maybe that fact contributed, but I would have very few good thi</span>
  <span id="freeText9226554127713004566" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"So, this is me, all of me, forever. No more looking back. No more regrets. From now on, vampire girl--" he lowered his head, brushing his lips across my skin "--I'm all yours."</i>
</b><br /><br />I promise no spoilers for this book but it would be impossible to review <i>The Forever Song</i> without giving away some things from the previous books. In my opinion, <u>this final installment is the weakest</u>. I thought the second book was a hard one to follow, so maybe that fact contributed, but I would have very few good things to say about this if it wasn't Jackal - who is actually one of my favourite YA paranormal characters and I so hope he gets his own spin-off (which looks quite likely).<br /><br /><b>So... what's up with all the angsting?</b><br /><br />I've known from the start that these books are quite dark, dreary and full of drama, but that's kind of what I liked about them. I liked reading about Allison's moral struggles and how she came to terms with being a monster and learned to embrace both sides of who she is. I liked reading about her relationship with Zeke and the convincing way the author depicted problems faced in a human/vampire relationship. I liked Kanin. And I LOVED the comic relief offered by Jackal's bitingly sarcastic sense of humour. But the latter was one of only two things that remained consistent with this last book. The other being the grittiness and vivid gory details.<br /><br />The first book in this series - <i>The Immortal Rules</i> - is an introduction to the world and characters. It's also slower than the other two and focuses on the changes in Allison's life and the way she adapts to them. The second book - <i>The Eternity Cure</i> - is much better. It's a complex, well-plotted story that mixes fast-paced action with humour, and nail-biting tension with romance. It's one of those books that just ticks every box. It excites, it surprises, it holds your attention. This last book isn't like that, in my opinion. It's <u>416 pages long</u> and about 80% of that is about <b>Allison and Zeke's romantic angst</b>. And maybe I wouldn't mind so much if they didn't go round and round in the same circles.<br /><br /><b>There are very few surprises.</b><br /><br />The plot was exactly as I expected it to be, in between copious amounts of vampire love drama. In fact, there is only one thing that happens near the end which I would consider a "surprise" and even that isn't particularly difficult to see coming - especially when you remind yourself that something dramatic has to happen at the climax. I keep saying it but without Jackal, this book would have been very disappointing. It's also, in part, an extremely long meditation on what it means to be a monster and how to be a vampire without choosing to become evil. Which is basically what the entire first book was about - why did we need to cover this again? <u>It was like de ja fucking angst.</u><br /><br /><b>The stuff I did actually like:</b><br /><br /><u>Gritty details:</u> Kagawa seems to be really good at this. This series, despite the age of the characters, often feels like a set of adult books because the author isn't afraid to <i>go there</i> and she never skimps on the details. I don't know about her Fey books, but this series is very gory and bloody... in horrific detail, at times. Which may or may not be your thing, but it works well for me. It also suits the dark, depressing setting and general feel of the novel - this is not a nice world and Kagawa isn't about to let you forget it.<br /><br /><u>Jackal:</u> Have I mentioned that I like him? Oops ;) But Jackal is just 100% the kind of character I like. He's witty, sarcastic and yeah, a bit of an asshole too. I can't help it; I love multilayered characters that are neither all good or all bad. And I think it's great when an author can take a character who does bad things but manages to make you love them anyway. I cannot tell you how much I would love a spin-off series featuring Jackal. <br /><br /><b>I would still recommend this series for fans of YA paranormal dystopias/romances.</b> These books are still very much worth reading - everyone deserves a bit of Jackal in their lives - but I think the trilogy peaked with the second book. Three stars, for me, is a positive rating and I can't deny that even at its weakest points, this series delivers enough drama, action and gore to keep readers interested. <br /><br /><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.leafmarks.com/emilymay" rel="nofollow noopener">Leafmarks</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://mycountryheart.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9226554127713004566" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer4285210686870979724"><b>After reading:</b><br/><br/>NOOOO IT'S OVER, NOOOOOOoooo.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396203302ra/9101392.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well, I am sad to see this series come to an end. I really enjoyed it.<br/><br/><i>The Forever Song</i> is a good conclusion to the trilogy, over all––as thrilling, action-packed, and emotional as the two books that preceded it. There were a few things that didn't quite work for me, and I'm still trying to decide how I feel about the ending ... But over all, it was worth the wait.<br/><br/>Full review coming soon!<br/><br/><b>Before reading:</b><br/><br/>The Forever Song?<br/><br/>THIS IS THE SONG THAT NEVER ENDS, Y</span>
  <span id="freeText4285210686870979724" style="display:none"><b>After reading:</b><br><br>NOOOO IT'S OVER, NOOOOOOoooo.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396203302ra/9101392.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, I am sad to see this series come to an end. I really enjoyed it.<br><br><i>The Forever Song</i> is a good conclusion to the trilogy, over all––as thrilling, action-packed, and emotional as the two books that preceded it. But over all, it was worth the wait.<br><br>Full review coming soon!<br><br><b>Before reading:</b><br><br>The Forever Song?<br><br>THIS IS THE SONG THAT NEVER ENDS, YES IT GOES ON AND ON MY FRIENDS, SOME PEOPLE STARTED SINGING IT NOT KNOWING WHAT IT WAS, AND THEY'LL CONTINUE SINGING IT FOREVER JUST BECAUSE THIS IS THE SONG THAT NEVER ENDS, YES IT GOES ON AND ON MY FRIENDS .... <br><br><b>Update 11/15/13:</b><br><br>Oh dear lord, it doesn't come out until April 29th, 2014. NOOOO.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383996894ra/6736914.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421760i/838306._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380420706ra/834868.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Update 3/13/14:</b> OOOOH A COVER. It's pretty. <br><br>Also <a href="https://www.netgalley.com/catalog/show/id/43046" rel="nofollow noopener">it's on NetGalley</a>! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394760756ra/8902332.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Update (3/16/14):</b> I GOT AN ARC. YAAAAAAY. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394249319ra/8828255.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So yeah, I will be reading this very soon. (Someone hold me, I'm scared.)</span>

<div id="review_904781411" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/904781411" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/904781411?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=blah-romance">blah-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring">boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=cheesy">cheesy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=rubbish">rubbish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=teens-saving-the-world">teens-saving-the-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring-crap-hero">boring-crap-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring-main-characters">boring-main-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=ugh">ugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=whiny-annoying-blah-heroine">whiny-annoying-blah-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer904781411" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14695268102033764039"><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/>An unremarkable end to an unremarkable series. <br/><br/>-<i>The Forever Song</i> mostly consisted of Allison walking, snarling, feeling sorry for herself, baring her fangs, making cheesy promises of revenge, and inner monologuing… And the rest of the story was made up of generic fight scenes.<br/><br/>-I hated Allison's character, she was such a crappy heroine. It pissed me off how her whole world revolved around a guy. She lost all her morals and turned into a heartless cow all because she thought she lost her l</span>
  <span id="freeText14695268102033764039" style="display:none"><b>Spoilers</b><br /><br />An unremarkable end to an unremarkable series. <br /><br />-<i>The Forever Song</i> mostly consisted of Allison walking, snarling, feeling sorry for herself, baring her fangs, making cheesy promises of revenge, and inner monologuing… And the rest of the story was made up of generic fight scenes.<br /><br />-I hated Allison's character, she was such a crappy heroine. It pissed me off how her whole world revolved around a guy. She lost all her morals and turned into a heartless cow all because she thought she lost her love interest, it was pathetic that her behaviour and ethics hinged on the fate of a boy.<br /><br />-I got tired of Allison talking about her Hunger and the Monster inside of her, I think it was meant to make her seem badass and dangerous but it just came across as annoying and silly. <br /><br />-Where were all the secondary female characters? There were none. Allison was always around guys (Jackal, Kanin, Zeke, Sarran) — she didn't have a SINGLE conversation with another female. Allison's vampire family was male, the soldiers were male, the doctors were male, the mayor was male — why couldn't one of them have been female?<br />In total, there was less than a page's worth of dialogue from other female characters that weren't Allison - I'm being generous calling them characters since they were pretty much non-characters.<br />She didn't have one strong female influence or relationship in her life. It seems like most YA authors have decided that the only story worth telling about a girl is one which revolves around boys. Ugh.<br /><br />-Allison and Jackal's bickering got really boring after a while, it just went on and on. I think it was meant to be funny or something but it was irritating having to read them bitch at each other over and over again.<br /><br />-Zeke was normal and sweet (if a bit boring) in the first two books, but he turned into the typical cold, emo, nobody-understands-me, I'm-so-tortured YA hero. It was nauseating.<br /><br />All in all, I wasn't impressed. Allison was insufferable, Zeke was awful, the story was repetitive and dull, and worst of all there were no secondary female characters. I won't be reading any future Julie Kagawa books. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14695268102033764039" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3589484486" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3589484486" />
    <a title="Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40997852-nicole"><img alt="Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605132719p2/40997852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3589484486?book_show_action=true">Oct 10, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nicole" href="/user/show/40997852-nicole">Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20733621-the-forever-song">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40997852-nicole?shelf=2020">2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40997852-nicole?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40997852-nicole?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3589484486" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6904279473543004649">This is a spoiler-free review for the whole trilogy. It'll be short since I can't say much without revealing the plot of the sequels. <br/><br/>I loved <i>Blood of Eden</i>. I have been dropping far too many YA trilogies and series (even if I liked them) but this one kept me interested to finish it in less than a year (again something unusual but I did learn not to wait a year to read a released sequel...). <br/><br/><b>If you're looking for a YA combining fantasy in a dystopian real world setting and has the good old memora</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6904279473543004649" style="display:none">This is a spoiler-free review for the whole trilogy. It'll be short since I can't say much without revealing the plot of the sequels. <br /><br />I loved <i>Blood of Eden</i>. I have been dropping far too many YA trilogies and series (even if I liked them) but this one kept me interested to finish it in less than a year (again something unusual but I did learn not to wait a year to read a released sequel...). <br /><br /><b>If you're looking for a YA combining fantasy in a dystopian real world setting and has the good old memorable YA feels... this is for you. </b><br />To me, the new YA releases, after 2016, are fun.. but mostly forgettable. I enjoy a book, move on to another, forget about it the next day. Meanwhile, I can still vividly remember YAs released before that if they 4-5 stars read. <br />On the other hand, several old YA pales in front of the new more exciting ones. They have so many cliches that new authors learned to avoid. <br />I'm glad to report this is a hella good trilogy that made me feel nostalgic and cozy -it's something I am familiar with all while being new in its own ways. <br /><br /><br /><b>If you're looking for a fun YA trilogy but unsure what to read since this genre isn't your thing anymore... this is for you.</b><br />You know this phase when someone feels too old for YA and that's why they made NA, the age difference is not big but at the same time enough to severely scrutinize the characters? <br />Anyway, for a while, I wasn't liking YA one bit. They all were the same color to me. The Folk of the Air was A HIT. Yet, I read the book, sure it's fun, carried on with my life. I tried several books but I just couldn't <i>connect</i> with the characters anymore. Until I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10215349.The_Immortal_Rules__Blood_of_Eden___1_" title="The Immortal Rules (Blood of Eden, #1) by Julie Kagawa" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Rules</a>. No, it wasn't a perfect book (and even in my review of it I wasn't sold yet) but I liked the characters. A lot. And I wanted to read the sequel ASAP. The next thing I knew, I was looking for more old YA I missed, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/764347.Unwind__Unwind___1_" title="Unwind (Unwind, #1) by Neal Shusterman" rel="nofollow noopener">Unwind</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6342491.The_Demon_King__Seven_Realms___1_" title="The Demon King (Seven Realms, #1) by Cinda Williams Chima" rel="nofollow noopener">The Demon King</a>, etc. and guess what? I was enjoying this genre again. <br /><br /><br /><b>If you're an avid YA reader and looking for a fun read with three-dimensional characters and a fast-paced plot... this is for you.</b><br />I smiled, I laughed, I cried, and I felt many emotions reading this trilogy. I know it'll always have a special place in my heart. I wouldn't go as far as saying one of my favorites but I truly loved it. It's those kinds of books that I have been struggling to find. I read over dozens of novels this year and yet how many can I truly say I remember and I still feel fond of? Not even 10.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>So why this trilogy?</u>
</b><br />- kickass east Asian heroine<br />- the most adorable love interest, I felt like he wasn't necessary in the first book but in the second? I fell in love with him. He'so damn cute and good-hearted. My heart simply twists now that I think about him. He truly cared about Allie and always supported her and held her back.<br />- awesome and cool secondary characters, Jackal, anyone? I also liked Kanin and how he was portrayed as a mentor to Allie.<br />- reading about a plague in the midst of the coronavirus epidemic? and a cure that made zombie-like creatures... *shudders* good thing we don't have vampires to make that kind of cure...<br />- fast-paced plot, the first chapter is usually a bit slow but IT'S THE FIRST CHAPTER OKAY? And then the book kicks off. <br /><br /><br />I wouldn't say this book is perfect, I won't go into details about the first two but the second was great enough for me to ignore those shortcomings and give it 5 shining stars.<br /><br />I'm not sure if this book or the first one is the weakest in this trilogy. While <i>The Forever Song</i> was very enjoyable, but it sadly wasn't perfect. The conclusion was satisfying and it made sense. Not completely predictable yet not shocking either (some parts you're probably going to see coming). It seems suitable however so you won't be disappointed. We had some cliche dialogues, which I dsliked, (or maybe this is just old me?). The writing was sometimes odd as in Allie using too formal language to address some characters in her head? I won't say any more about to not spoil anything. <br /><br />After reading the second book which had a lot going on, this one solely focused on one mission. Which is understandable but I also wanted more. Not for the mission to prolong any longer, God no. But maybe it would've been more of a zig-zag mission instead of a straight line? <br /><br />Overall, I recommend this series for its characters, where secondary ones sometimes outshone Allie, the addicting plot, and the memorable story. It might not be perfect not the best out there but it's definitely worth reading.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6904279473543004649" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4521206802260977344"><br/><br/><i><b><blockquote>“I am proud of you, Allison Sekemoto,” he whispered “Whatever you decide, whatever path you choose to take, I hope that you will remain the same girl I met that night in the rain. The one decision for which I have no regrets.”</blockquote></b> </i><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1470503817i/19936138.jpg' width='500' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><u>It is always difficult to start a review when you have so many feelings about a book, especially in a trilogy or saga, but I think at the same time or at least in my case, I can express better my opinions and so I can calm down myself a little too lol .</u><br/><br/><br/>We can see a very di</span>
  <span id="freeText4521206802260977344" style="display:none"><br><br><i><b><blockquote>“I am proud of you, Allison Sekemoto,” he whispered “Whatever you decide, whatever path you choose to take, I hope that you will remain the same girl I met that night in the rain. The one decision for which I have no regrets.”</blockquote></b> </i><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1470503817i/19936138.jpg" width="500" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>It is always difficult to start a review when you have so many feelings about a book, especially in a trilogy or saga, but I think at the same time or at least in my case, I can express better my opinions and so I can calm down myself a little too lol .</u><br><br><br>We can see a very different <b>
  <i>Allie</i>
</b> this time, in her trip to Eden, along with Kanin and Jackal, after the death of Zeke, she is determined to leave the feelings of the past behind of her and make way for her demon part, which dominates her completely in the early chapters of history , thus becoming a more dangerous vampire.<br>I really liked this change in her, although clearly the change is due to a very sad thing it has happened in her life, I think Allie had to experience it to really understand what being a vampire means, and what are the real consequences about it .<br><br><br><u>I think of the three books this is in my opinion, that more action scenes has, made me feel as if the characters were in real danger constantly, causing the plot catch me and I've want to read on to discover who lives or who dies.</u><br><br><br>When you feel so attached to the plot, when you don't know what is happening or will happen, and even so continuous to the reading, it is totally merit of the writer, and in this case as I mentioned Julie Kagawa is amazing doing it!. Now I'm sure that will not take anything in deciding to reading a new book of hers :).<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470504099ra/19936213.gif" width="500" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“If we are talking about choice and regret, what has happened cannot be undone. And dwelling on the past changes nothing. You will only drive yourself to insanity if you do.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><br><br><u>Has left me so happy that I feel very good about each of the characters, absolutely all have grown much and I'll miss everyone.</u><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Jackal</i>
</b> is so funny, outgoing and always saying what he thinks, although the most unexpected things lol, he has no filter. I love him so much, is a character without waste, I think I easily I would read a whole book about him. I am very pleased with how everything has ended for him, I would have liked something else, not gonna lie, but it was very fine.<br><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You know,” Jackal said, kicking a rabid in the face, sending it reeling, “it seems that whenever I’m with you, I’m constantly fighting my way into places I really don’t want to be. The sewers, the Prince’s tower, a bloody freaking church.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><br><br><b>
  <i>Kanin</i>
</b> always be definitely my favorite character!<br>This master vampire has won my heart, it is a noble being and his dispocision to help others is always worth noting, I think that the plot would not have been the same without him, is a character, essential for that history has finished as just end .<br><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Even I can't believe what happened to Kanin, I knew someone was going to die, but did not want that had to be him :(. I still don't accept it. I've cried like a baby.. #TeamKaninforever! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“No.” Kanin’s voice was suddenly hard, terrifying. “You are simply using your demon to hide from what you really feel. Because you are afraid of what that means, that it might be painful. It is far easier to be a monster than to confront the truth.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><br> <br><u>I can't tell much more without make this a big spoiler haha, but <b><u>I CRY LIKE A BABY!</u></b> .<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462332249ra/18982996.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>What I want you to know is that there has been an incredible journey, since Allie was turned into a vampire until the end, although there have been little things that don't make it a favorite for me, there are thousands who I will always remember. Absolutely brilliant plot, charming characters that you gonna love, undoubtedly, others that you gonna hate with all your soul (as Sarren, I add, is an amazing villain), many survival , especially too many surprises and strong feelings!. So if you ask me if I would recommend this trilogy to you, I would answer <b>ALWAYS!</b> :)</u><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1919732571161076271">Rating Clarification: 3.5 stars<br/><br/><b>This series is definitely a MUST READ.   <span id="freeText1919732571161076271" style="display:none">Rating Clarification: 3.5 stars<br /><br /><b>This series is definitely a MUST READ. These books are constant page turners, gripping, enthralling and exhilarating.</b> <br /><br />Personally, I think that this third installment had too much action and no down time. Part of what made me love the first installment so much is that it had the perfect combination of both action and narrative, the action is perfectly fine , but the down time makes that action better, gives it more tension and also with the slow moments we can have time to reflect, assimilate and feel. In my opinion we miss profoundness with so much action.<br /><br />Despite the fact that is categorized young –adult and the characters are 17-18 years old, they could perfectly be older, there is no teen drama here, the books would have work just as well having Allie and Zeke being in their 20s.<br /><br />As the way the book ended, we could have a Jackal spin-off series!<br /><br /><b>Audiobook</b>  The narrator <b>Therese Plummer</b> does a <u>terrific job</u>. She gives the perfect tone and <u>strength</u> to the story and the characters. She unquestionably <u>improves the narrative</u>. I <u>definitely recommend listening</u> to this audio-book edition instead of reading the book. <br /><br /><b>The overall feeling of the series is really good, excellent</b>. It has a <b>fascinating set of characters, a compelling story line and a great universe. <br />READ IT!</b><br /><br /><br />My Reviews in the <u>Blood of Eden</u> Series:<br />Book 0.5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1229029317" rel="nofollow noopener">Dawn of Eden</a><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1228896866?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Rules</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230131130" rel="nofollow noopener">Eternity Cure</a><br />Book 2.5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230131614?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Zeke's Letter to Allie</a> <br />Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230131438?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Forever Song</a></span>

<div id="review_1040612914" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1040612914" />
    <a title="Dorreh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh"><img alt="Dorreh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565727363p2/22599584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1040612914?book_show_action=true">Aug 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dorreh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dorreh" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh">Dorreh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1040612914" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11717626877491761910">The last book in this series was great. It followed up on all the elements and gruesome details that enchanted me so very much in the first book. The element of surprise and change that occurred in the love relationship, although foreseeable, was amply believable and well portrayed. <br/><br/>I can't really complain because I did love everything about this book, and I think it ended well. Kanins death was a necessary evil to heighten the drama, a symbolic representation of sacrifice for the greater good. </span>
  <span id="freeText11717626877491761910" style="display:none">The last book in this series was great. It followed up on all the elements and gruesome details that enchanted me so very much in the first book. The element of surprise and change that occurred in the love relationship, although foreseeable, was amply believable and well portrayed. <br /><br />I can't really complain because I did love everything about this book, and I think it ended well. Kanins death was a necessary evil to heighten the drama, a symbolic representation of sacrifice for the greater good. It was dramatic, realistic, and vastly emotional.<br /><br />But in general my favorite thing in books two and three was the siblings love hate relationship. The shades of gray in every person (or in this case vampire) made a great influence on the way you looked at the story. I guess what captured me most was the touches of reality signified in this fantasy tale. The only thing that prevents me from giving this book a full 5 is the extension of Zekes moping period was a little too long, the whining on his behalf set me off a little. I mean yeah I get the whole guilt and despair, but he sounded more whiny than miserable to me. But like I said, can't complain, as I really enjoyed reading this series. It made my blood boil, and at the same my heart wrench for it's characters and events.</span>

<div id="review_625074014" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/625074014" />
    <a title="Lisa RC" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7053867-lisa-rc"><img alt="Lisa RC" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1414954997p2/7053867.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/625074014?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa RC" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa RC" href="/user/show/7053867-lisa-rc">Lisa RC</a>
      </span>

          marked it as to-read

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer625074014" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16545274714586347447"><b>January 2014 Update </b> <br/>That cover... a little too girly for me. Anyone else see the infinity sign the birds make? HAHA. GET IT? <b> FOREVER</b> made by birds = song. Cool stuff. <br/><br/><b>The Forever Song</b> <br/>I can't help but think: <br/>Crazy Sarren thinks song = scream. So forever song = everlasting torture. <br/>But then again, the title is so darn beautiful, I'm crying just reading it. <br/><br/>Let's start with why I love this series: <br/>Everytime I read a Blood of Eden novel, all I think is grey. The setting is so dark and dreary and </span>
  <span id="freeText16545274714586347447" style="display:none"><b>January 2014 Update </b> <br />That cover... a little too girly for me. Anyone else see the infinity sign the birds make? HAHA. GET IT? <b> FOREVER</b> made by birds = song. Cool stuff. <br /><br /><b>The Forever Song</b> <br />I can't help but think: <br />Crazy Sarren thinks song = scream. So forever song = everlasting torture. <br />But then again, the title is so darn beautiful, I'm crying just reading it. <br /><br />Let's start with why I love this series: <br />Everytime I read a Blood of Eden novel, all I think is grey. The setting is so dark and dreary and I can't understand WHY I like something like that. Like, I love books with...glamour. Or at least, some colour. So I guess dark series is the first impressive one I've read. <br /><br />The characters. Not sure about you, but I love all the characters, even the crazy ones. <br />Stick: that @^&amp;$%#. It takes an impressive author to make you HATE someone so much. I liked it more when Allison wanted to kill him (I mean, it proves that she too, is a flawed character). Even when he died, I was happy. <br />Serran: crazy psychopath. Again, takes an awesome writer to make you hate this guy. But then again, it's understandable because he was tortured by humans. <br />Zeke: No words for him, but I really want to KNOW him more. I feel like he the character with the least depth, especially for a main character. <br />Kanin: I keep on thinking of this old guy when they mention him. But he's so...strong. Morally. You get tortured and nearly die from the Hunger, but still manage to come back. (I thought he had a thing for Allison after he bit her). He's such a nice guy. Gosh, I'm crying. <br />Jackal: best bad guy ever. He's all witty and makes the smartest remarks, but at the same time, he knows when to let go. Reminds me of Puck from the Iron Fae series. Other than the fact he killed Zeke's groupies and wants vampires to rule the world, I think he's a decent character. Maybe it's wrong for me to think this way, but I think James and Allison sounds like a nice pair :) <br />Allison: definitely flawed, and that's what I like about her. She doesn't deny the monster inside of her, and knows how to tame it. There's something about her that makes her unique. She's the most human of them all. Great female lead. <br />YAY VAMPIRE GIRL AND PREACHER BOY. <br />The writing style: yay description and small font! <br /><br /><b>What I hope will happen</b> <br />Allison (A): Let go of Zeke! <br />Sarren (S): I like to hear him sing!! <br />Kanin (K): This is between me and you. Let go of the kid. <br />Jackel (J): Oh... we're so doomed. Oh. Since we're doomed. HAHA, guys. I'm switching sides...again! That makes me a triple agent. <br />S: Now that we're at Eden, we just need to enter. [Uses Zeke's DNA to get in]. MWAHAHA. Now I'm going to release that virus after a destroy their labs. First, I have to kill this little bird. <br />[Stabs Zeke] <br />Zeke: "Sings" <br />A: NOOO! <br />[S runs off and K follows] <br />A: oh Zeke. I love you! <br />Z: Change me. Please. <br />A: but...but... <br />Z: I love you so much. I want to be with you. Make it quick. <br />[Transforms him]. <br />Z: Ahh... feeling good already. Let's go kick his bum <br />[Finds S, who happens to kill K for good. S gets captured and used for experiments again through the work of A and Z. Somewhere halfway, Jackel changes sides again]. <br />At the end, the two of them + Jackel are cured! <br /><br />The Forever Song. Can't wait. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16545274714586347447" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
