<div id="review_776427314" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/776427314" />
    <a title="Faye, la Patata" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7650833-faye-la-patata"><img alt="Faye, la Patata" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557835753p2/7650833.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/776427314?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Faye, la Patata" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Faye, la Patata" href="/user/show/7650833-faye-la-patata">Faye, la Patata</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer776427314" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1993852750080854304"><b>
  <i>
    <u>RANT AHEAD</u>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><strong>As much as I liked this series as a whole, I could not be any happier that Allison's whining has ended.</strong> I know that looks very, very weird on paper, but if you read the books from start to finish, you should know that <em>angst</em> is pretty much the main character's trademark. You cannot have the name <em>Allison Sekemoto</em> without <i>angst</i> attached to it like an octopus with its brutal eight-tentacled crush (thank you, Khanh). They go together, hand-in-hand, never without the other.<br/><br/>But se</span>
  <span id="freeText1993852750080854304" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <u>RANT AHEAD</u>
  </i>
</b><br><br><strong>As much as I liked this series as a whole, I could not be any happier that Allison's whining has ended.</strong> I know that looks very, very weird on paper, but if you read the books from start to finish, you should know that <em>angst</em> is pretty much the main character's trademark. You cannot have the name <em>Allison Sekemoto</em> without <i>angst</i> attached to it like an octopus with its brutal eight-tentacled crush (thank you, Khanh). They go together, hand-in-hand, never without the other.<br><br>But seriously, all that silly stuff aside, I really am glad the series is over, and it ended in a rather positive note. No loose ends (that I can think of, but then again, I was too busy raging about Allison's whining to even bother about plotholes), nothing bad to grieve or rage over. <strong>In a way, it was a satisfying ending to one of the darkest, grimmest, and bleakest vampire novels in Young Adult that I've ever read. It sent chills up in my spine, it kept me on my toes, it made my stomach do back-flips.</strong><br><br><strong>However... like the book, it was not all rainbows and sunshine. I found a LOT of problems here.</strong> Most are probably subjective, and may depend on the person's patience and perspective, but they remained issues for me and played a large part in my not completely enjoying it. Call me nitpicky if you wish, I don't care; the fact remains that while reading, there were times when it made me want to fling it out the window, and times when I'd put it aside because it frustrated me too much.<br><br><strong>Exhibit A: ALLISON</strong><br><br><em>Evidence 1: She is angsty.</em><br><br><strong>As an overall character, Allison is pretty cool. She's not one-dimensional and all and has shown a lot of depth and complexity especially with regards to her humanity.</strong> I appreciate how in the previous books, she was torn between fighting for her human side and embracing what she has become. It's that kind of thinking that gives leeway to many philosophical ideas that people like Socrates, Kant, and Déscartes are known for. <strong>However, since book 1, and unfortunately until book 3, she has this tendency to do it in such an angsty and whiny manner.</strong> Which is not really a bad thing, really! Angst, if done right, and if done in reasonable amounts, can be fun to read (come on, don't look at me that way! We all need to read a bit of drama every once in a while!).<br><br><strong>However, what I didn't like about her was how she did it too much. Angst here, angst there, angst everywhere.</strong> It felt never-ending. I had this problem before, especially in book 2, which was pretty much an angst-fest in a nutshell, but I hoped it would end here. Like I said, there's nothing wrong with it per se<strong>, but if you already resolved this problem pages ago,</strong> and if someone already assured you that what you're whining about is nothing to wallow over, <strong>and you still continue to do it ten pages later,</strong> then <strong>yes</strong>, we <strong>do</strong> have a <strong>problem</strong>.<br><br>Take this quote for example:<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"Everything that's happened - from New Covington, to Eden, to here - is your fault, vampire girl. Jebbadiah is dead, because you couldn't save him. Kanin was tortured and nearly killed, because you had to see if Stick was all right, and he betrayed you both to the Prince. Everyone in Eden is going to die, because you let Sarren get away." His eyes glittered with hate. "And I... I'm dead, because you came into my life, and I was stupid  enough to fall in love with a monster. You killed me, Allie. Not Sarren. I'm a vampire now, because of you."</em>
  <br>
  <br>
  <em>Every word, every accusation, hit like a knife, slicing me open. But the last nearly dropped me to my knees. Tears blurred my vision, and I turned from Zeke, slumping against a section of roof that had fallen in. My fault. Jackal had been right. It was my fault that Zeke was dead, my fault for everything.</em>
</blockquote><br><br><strong>ASDASDASAGGDFGHFGJDFHDSG</strong><br><br>This part was especially frustrating to me because pages and pages before that, Allison was wallowing in self-pity about her beloved's "death", and Jackal's snide comments about it were not helping. Kanin then told her that there is nothing to worry about, it wasn't her fault, it was Sarren, don't worry, everything else that happened wasn't your fault at all, etc. etc., which, thankfully, comforted her (and shut her up a little).<strong>
  <em> So why are we going over this drama again a few pages later?!</em>
</strong> I like angst, but not if you keep repeating the same thing over and over and over like a broken record.<br><br><em>Evidence 2: She has derp moments. </em><br><br>Many times throughout the book, I hated how Allison would showcase special cases of stupidity. Imagine this: you are about to fight what could <em>potentially</em> be the hardest battle in your life in a remote citadel in Old Chicago. You are wounded and surrounded by raiders who ooze with raging testosterone. You know you need your strength, and you know you need your friends' help as well. But look! The stairs collapsed! Uh-oh. You're cut off from the rest of your team. You're alone. And the bad guy is just right in front of you, very likely sharpening its fangs to sink into your throat. Of course, you'd wait for your team, right? This could possibly be your last chance; heck, <em>you</em> could be humanity's <em>last chance</em>, so it's better to make it worth it. Your team tells you to wait for them. They'll be right with you.<br><br>What are your choices?<br><br>A.) Wait for your team to arrive.<br>B.) Fuck the rest, you go alone. Surely your wounded state is enough to fight and <em>defeat</em> the madman ahead.<br><br>So yeah, you can pretty much guess what Allison did in a nutshell. The following isn't exactly what transpired, but that was the gist of it:<br><br><strong>Kanin and Jackal</strong>: We've been separated. Do NOT go against the enemy alone!<br><strong>Allison</strong>: (sees sensitive object that reminded her of Zeke) (fills with blind fury) Must... kill... Sarren...<br><strong>Kanin and Jackal</strong>: Wait for us there! We repeat, don't go on your own!<br><strong>Allison</strong>: Must... kill... Sarren...<br><strong>Kanin and Jackal</strong>: We will face him toge---<br><strong>Allison</strong>: Must... kill... SAAAARREEEEN (runs to enemy... alone)<br><p>
  <img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395842732i/9051287._SX540_.png" width="344" height="341" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><em>Evidence 3:</em> <em>She likes cheese.</em><br><br>Ugh. <strong>Okay, this is <em>extremely</em> nitpicky of me, and I apologize if you think I'm being overly shallow about this, but I seriously cannot help it. There are times Allison says a lot of great quotes, but there are also times they're full of WTF.</strong> Like, whoa, was this lifted from a Nicolas Cage action movie or something? Did you watch some corny chick flicks and subconsciously etched a cringe-worthy quote or two, Allison? So many of them made me roll my sockets, and some of them even made me put the book down and stare at it with judging eyes.<br><br>Examples:<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"Watch me, Zeke. I'll send your killer to hell, and I'll smile while I'm doing it."</em>
</blockquote><br>Did you watch too many Die Hard movies, Allie?<br><blockquote>
  <em>"Sarren is not going to win. I am not giving our forever to that sick bastard. this isn't over yet.</em>
</blockquote><br><em>Our</em> forever? Really?<br><br><strong>Exhibit B: Zeke</strong><br><br><em>Evidence: He's Allison 2.0</em><br><br>No, really.<strong> He is</strong>. As was implied in Book 2, he died and was resurrected by Sarren as a vampire. When he comes around later on, he becomes as angsty as Allison. This wouldn't have been so bad, if he had something new to angst about. But unfortunately, what he whined here, Allison already whined about them in Book 1: regarding retaining one's humanity and giving in to the Hunger that is prevalent in Vampires. It's fine the first time, the second time, the third... but if you keep doing it over and over and over (again), it just gets <em>real</em> exhausting, dude. Like, seriously. I'm pretty sure you have better stuff to do than cry the same crocodile tears.<br><br>This is what usually consists of Zeke and Allison's conversations:<br><br><strong>Zeke</strong>: You must kill me, Allie. I can't live as a Vampire. I'll only kill those I love!<br><strong>Allie</strong>: No, stay with me! You can control it! I'll teach you how!<br><strong>Zeke</strong>: Okay. I'm glad you're there. (5 minutes later) Oh, Allison. I can't do it. Sooner or later, I <em>will</em> kill people I love!<br><strong>Allie</strong>: I'm here for you! I won't let you do that! I lost you once, I won't lose you again!<br><strong>Zeke</strong>: Okay. Seriously, thanks for being there. (5 minutes later) Oh, god. I can't stand with myself if I do kill innocents! I've done it before, Allie! I'll only do it again!<br><strong>Allie</strong>: Zeke, you can do it. Don't you want <em>our </em>forever?<br><strong>Zeke</strong>: Yeah, okay. Love you.<br><br><strong>It's like being in a motherfucking twilight zone.</strong><br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364575ra/716294.gif" width="245" height="182" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>EXHIBIT C: THAT RANDOM TWIST</strong><br><br><em></em><em>Evidence: Its very existence.</em><br><br>Okay, I won't spoil what that twist is, because that will only ruin the entire book and series for you. It happened near the end, and instead of being shocked or overjoyed, I was simply... <strong>dumbfounded</strong>. Yup, that's right. I just sat there, read the scene again to make sure I was reading it right, and scratched my ebony head<strong>. I love twists and all, but this one just came off as seriously random, like, it sprung out of nowhere without any warning.</strong> Usually I like twists with a bit of foreshadowing and with a bit of background already shown, but this one? Where the hell did it come from? How someone becomes (X) was never mentioned in any of the books and it felt so convenient to place it there as the be-all end-all solution to the problem. Yup, it felt convenient to me. Although this is just perhaps a difference of perspectives.<br><br>Although to be honest, there were a lot of good stuff too. They are the following:<br><br><strong>THE GOOD</strong><br><br><strong>1.)</strong> Jackal. God, he was brilliant. He's my favorite character of the whole series for me. Yeah he can be brutal and merciless and sarcastic, but boy, he says the best quotes and plus, he's sees beyond himself. That's what I liked about him the most. He's practical and he sees the greater picture, unlike Allison who, I felt, is sometimes stuck in her own little bubble.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"Does it matter?" asked Jackal behind us. "Who cares what he's up to? He can be planning to fill the world with puppies, and I'm still going to rip the shriveled black heart from his chest and shove it down his throat until he chokes on it."</em>
</blockquote><br><br>This is why I loves ya.<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>Raising his head, he bellowed into the room: "Hey, minions! Daddy's home and he's not happy! But because I'm such a nice guy, I'm going to give you a choice. You can make it easy for yourself and blow your brains out right now, or I can slowly twist your head around until it pops right off your neck. Your move!"</em>
</blockquote><br><br>Ohhh, you're so sexy smexy. Sizzle!<br><br><blockquote>
  <em>"Oh, heads are going to roll for this. I'm going to set up a special lane and use their skulls for bowling balls."</em>
</blockquote><br><br>So especially funny, too!<br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394004315ra/8795217.gif" width="245" height="241" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>2.) </strong>It's absolutely atmospheric. Kagawa has serious talent for really making the world dark, grim, and dreary. We're given descriptions of the surroundings that really help us visualize <em>and feel</em> the bleakness of it all. Dead trees with equally dead humans hanging under the branches, humans handing from the ceiling with their intestines drooping out like pink snails, the dangerous feeling of Jackal's Citadel in Old Chicago, the hopelessness in Eden... she's really great for making you feel <em>you're there</em>. So kudos, Miss Kagawa!<br><br><strong>3.)</strong> Kanin. He's such a phenomenal character in and out. He helped create the world today and you can see he's trying his best to make up for it in ways that he can. He's pretty much everyone's beacon of light and standing foundation, and you just love him for it. He's so strong and vulnerable at the same time that you just want to hug him and whisper in his ear that everything will be alright.<br><br><b>OVERALL...</b><br><br><strong>I still stand with my opinion that this series is one of the best out there in YA about Vampires.</strong> They're not carebear at all and they're fear, dangerous, and deadly. They are truly presented as how they should be, and it posts very interesting points about humanity and being human. <strong>Allison and Zeke were not the strongest factors in this series for me, but the plot in general as well as  the side characters were absolutely fun to read.</strong> They were the ones who MADE this series for me enjoyable. Without them, I'm not sure I could stand the constant angst being thrown left and right. Overall, a good series. Recommended with reservations.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1993852750080854304" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hannah (The Curiouser &amp; Curiouser)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hannah (The Curiouser &amp; Curiouser)" href="/user/show/15749291-hannah-the-curiouser-curiouser">Hannah (The Curiouser &amp; Curiouser)</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692579147" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7431337558200179301">Updated 5/17/14.<br/><br/>One word.<br/><br/>Jackal.<br/><br/>I just freakin’ love Jackal.<br/><br/>Honestly, the only, <i>only</i> reason I gave this book a 3.5 out of 5 stars was because of Jackal and (somewhat) Kanin. And the fact that Sarren finally, <i>finally</i> dies in the best possible way.<br/><br/>Case in point (via the amazing Jackal):<br/><br/><pre>“Oh, isn’t that sweet,” came Jackal’s loud, mocking voice… “Let’s make goo-goo eyes at each other in the middle of a stinking corpse field, how very romantic.”</pre><br/><br/><pre>“Go ahead, tell him that everything is going to be fine.</pre></span>
  <span id="freeText7431337558200179301" style="display:none">Updated 5/17/14.<br><br>One word.<br><br>Jackal.<br><br>I just freakin’ love Jackal.<br><br>Honestly, the only, <i>only</i> reason I gave this book a 3.5 out of 5 stars was because of Jackal and (somewhat) Kanin. And the fact that Sarren finally, <i>finally</i> dies in the best possible way.<br><br>Case in point (via the amazing Jackal):<br><br><pre>“Oh, isn’t that sweet,” came Jackal’s loud, mocking voice… “Let’s make goo-goo eyes at each other in the middle of a stinking corpse field, how very romantic.”</pre><br><br><pre>“Go ahead, tell him that everything is going to be fine. All the meatsacks are perfectly content on their happy little island, Sarren has given up world destruction to raise kittens, and the magic wish fairy will wave her wand and turn shit to gold.”</pre><br><br><pre>“I’m still going to eat them. How much is going to depend on how seriously they piss me off by the time I get in there.”</pre><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400312756ra/9662326.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What made this book so good was Jackal’s role in it. He’s constantly there to tell Allie off and make witty remarks about the whole situation that makes one wonder why the whole series doesn’t revolve around him.<br><br>Allie, on the other hand . . .<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400312756ra/9662327.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On one hand, I like her that way. She’s pretty real, but there are times when it’s just like, the girl needs to get her crap together. This woe is me act is getting a little distasteful, and, honestly, I only cared to read about her in the hopes Jackal would tell her off in that delicious way that he does. I swear, if the world wasn’t about to s*** bricks even more so because of the insane Sarren, Allie would just fall apart. I get it. She loves Zeke. I really do. And I can’t blame her; he’s pretty great. But the second she’s not with him, Allie goes all ballistic, hormonal, whiny teenage vampire girl on us. And, you know what, fine. She’s entitled to that since she thinks he’s dead. TO AN EXTENT. But noooooo . . . instead, the first 1/3 of the book is wholly dedicated to her self-pity.<br><br>Never mind that the world is going:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400312641ra/9662253.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But never mind that little matter, Allie just wants to:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400312641ra/9662254.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400312641ra/9662255.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400312641ra/9662256.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>THE WHOLE 1/3 OF THE FREAKIN’ BOOK.<br><br>And then there’s Zeke. (I literally just sat here for a whole minute trying to remember what his name was.) I just don’t care about him. He’s boorrrriiinnnggggg. All I remember about him is that he broods for a good portion of the book, then makes out with Allie, then gets all mushy on me.<br><br>And then Jackal pops in, saves the day, and says:<br><br><pre>“Puppy, I am getting so tired of listening to you whine about this,” he snarled at Zeke. “This isn’t rocket science. If you don’t want to be a monster, don’t be a bloody monster! Be an uptight stick in the mud like Kanin. Be a self-righteous bleeding heart like Allison. Or you can stop agonizing about it and be a fucking monster.”</pre><br><br>YES.<br><br>The other character I loved was Kanin. He’s sooo . . . weird.<br><br>This whole family scenario Allie, Jackal, and Kanin have going on is a little strange, but I still loved it. For the past few books I felt that Kanin was a pretty interesting character, but in this one, well . . . all I can remember is that he’s playing the role of the tired father of two annoying children.<br><br>I swear, all of his lines revolved around, <i>Stop fighting you two, Hands and swords to yourselves, Allison and James,</i> or, my personal favorite, <i>Either you two stop bickering or, so help me, I’m turning this car around.</i><br><br>Book reviews can also be found here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://obsessivereads.wordpress.com/">http://obsessivereads.wordpress.com/</a><br><br>_______________________________________________________________________<br><br>Updated 1/23/14.<br><br>Look! LOOK!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1390490674l/17883441.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And it has the infinity symbol in the background!!!!!<br><br>OHMIGOSH. Still dead.<br><br>_______________________________________________________________________<br><br>Oh . . . the ending to the second book . . . OHHHHHHHHH . . . <br><br>Torture is in an author's nature, ISN'T IT? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432742ra/870335.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Gosh darn it . . . WHYYYYYYY???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432742ra/870336.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And that release date? WHAT IS THIS?! WHAT IS THIS UNKIND LIFE???<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413694ra/814904.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And now I'm like, I'm like . . . an emotional WRECK because I love these characters more than I should and ZEKE . . . NONONONONONONONONONONONONO <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432742ra/870337.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>. . . DOES NOT COMPUTE.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432742ra/870338.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And . . . and . . . and Kanin! And Jackel! I WANT MORE JACKEL! THE SARCASM AND WITTY PUNS ARE A MUST. <br>And I really, reaalllyyyy want more of Kanin. <span id="freeTextContainer8423533530760374822">I just finished this and...I feel numb. I can't believe its all actually over. The story has come to an end.<br/><br/>But what a wonderful end it was.<br/><br/>This series...oh man. I can't properly express my feelings for it. Just saying that I loved it isn't enough. It felt like this story reached into me and tore out my heart, patched it back together, tore it out all over again, and just kept repeating. But in the end, it left me feeling satisfied, even though we still lost a lot.<br/><br/>I'm unable to write anything el</span>
  <span id="freeText8423533530760374822" style="display:none">I just finished this and...I feel numb. I can't believe its all actually over. The story has come to an end.<br /><br />But what a wonderful end it was.<br /><br />This series...oh man. I can't properly express my feelings for it. Just saying that I loved it isn't enough. It felt like this story reached into me and tore out my heart, patched it back together, tore it out all over again, and just kept repeating. But in the end, it left me feeling satisfied, even though we still lost a lot.<br /><br />I'm unable to write anything else because my brain is still numb and my eyes keep tearing up, but I will end with this: Hey, Julie Kagawa? Your writing is amazing. This is not a new revelation, but I just have to keep repeating it because every time I finish one of your books, I'm left in awe. So thank you. And I hope you continue writing these amazing stories. I'm also hoping that you're planning on writing a spin-off series like you did with your Iron Fey series, and I know that may never happen, but...I'm going to continue hoping.<br /><br />Good bye Allison Sekemoto, the most bad ass mother fucking vampire I'll ever know.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9035290986968288444">The last book in the trilogy and I guess it was a satisfactory ending. All of the story lines were neatly tied up except maybe for Jackal and there is apparently the possibility that he may get his own spin off series which would be nice!<br/>Jackal was actually the best thing about this book. His sarcastic and humorous comments provided some lightness to an otherwise very heavy story. There was a lot of fighting and also a lot of angst about how hungry everyone was and whether a vampire had to be a </span>
  <span id="freeText9035290986968288444" style="display:none">The last book in the trilogy and I guess it was a satisfactory ending. All of the story lines were neatly tied up except maybe for Jackal and there is apparently the possibility that he may get his own spin off series which would be nice!<br />Jackal was actually the best thing about this book. His sarcastic and humorous comments provided some lightness to an otherwise very heavy story. There was a lot of fighting and also a lot of angst about how hungry everyone was and whether a vampire had to be a monster. Allie turned into rather tedious person, constantly rushing in to situations and then having to be saved by one of the others. <br />So the book had some faults but it did keep moving, it had lots of action and it rounded off the trilogy. I am glad I read it:)</span>

<div id="review_874283605" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/874283605" />
    <a title="Anne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1720620-anne"><img alt="Anne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415374035p2/1720620.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/874283605?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne" href="/user/show/1720620-anne">Anne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1720620-anne?shelf=mature-ya">mature-ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer874283605" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer376201858060899591">If you've been following these books, then I think you'll be happy with the final installment. It's a good solid ending to the Blood of Eden trilogy.<br/><br/><b>Warning: Spoilers for the previous books on the way!</b><br/><br/>It keeps the theme of the other books, in that vampires are not cuddly or misunderstood.<br/>Allie has been struggling to keep her humanity throughout the first two books, and with the help of her mentor Kanin, she's managed to keep from sucking people dry. Of course, it helped that she was in love with</span>
  <span id="freeText376201858060899591" style="display:none">If you've been following these books, then I think you'll be happy with the final installment. It's a good solid ending to the Blood of Eden trilogy.<br><br><b>Warning: Spoilers for the previous books on the way!</b><br><br>It keeps the theme of the other books, in that vampires are not cuddly or misunderstood.<br>Allie has been struggling to keep her humanity throughout the first two books, and with the help of her mentor Kanin, she's managed to keep from sucking people dry. Of course, it helped that she was in love with a human.<br>At the end of the last book, Sarren had captured Zeke, and left a video of Zeke being tortured to death just to screw with her. So it was no real surprise that when the story opens, Allie has gone a little off the deep end. She's still determined to stop Sarren from unleashing the virus that will wipe everyone off of the planet, but she's now on board with Jackal's version of how a vampire should act.<br><i>Chomp, chomp, chompin' on the humans...</i><br><br>Unfortunately, I can't say much else without giving major spoilers.<br>I can say that I was totally expecting most of what happened to, um...<i>happen</i>? But it didn't all play out exactly the way I thought it would.<br><br>My only complaint would be that I did occasionally get a tad annoyed by Allie's somewhat dry and crunchy inner thoughts. Sometimes (not always) her inner monologue seemed too formal. I mean, she's been traveling around with Kanin for a few books now, and yet she would still mentally refer to him as <i>The Master Vampire</i>. As in, <i>The master vampire looked over the city with an unreadable expression on his face.</i><br>*That's not a quote by the way, just an example.*<br>I mean, it just seemed like she should have said something more like,<i> Kanin had an unreadable expression on his face while he looked over the city.</i> <br>I don't think I'm explaining this right, but Allie used Kanin and Jackal's titles (the Raider King, the master vampire, my mentor, my brother) way too much for someone raised on the streets.<br><i>This whole paragraph doesn't really makes sense, does it? I really probably should just delete it, since it's just pretty much one bullshit complaint in an otherwise decent book, but I've already spent a good hunk of my time trying to figure out how to say this. I feel like I'm locked into it now.<br>Ugh. Don't you hate that?!</i><br>Anyhoo. Feel free to disregard my above brain fart, 'cause I can't bring myself to use the backspace key.<br><br>Again, if you liked the first two books, you'll like this one. This is the only thing I've read by Kagawa so far, but I'm sorta tempted to check out her Iron Fey series now.<br><br><i>
  <b>Thanks, NetGalley! I pinky swear this is an honest review. Blah, blah, blah...</b>
</i><br><br><div>
  <a href="http://www.addicted2heroines.com/2014/04/early-reviewthe-forever-song-blood-of.html" title="Addicted 2 Heroines" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412937777i/11444542.jpg" alt="Addicted 2 Heroines" width="100%" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</div></span>

<div id="review_860588854" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/860588854" />
    <a title="Reading Teen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3329955-reading-teen"><img alt="Reading Teen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1294347905p2/3329955.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/860588854?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Reading Teen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Reading Teen" href="/user/show/3329955-reading-teen">Reading Teen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer860588854" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7416649686551448594">Such an epic conclusion to an amazingly exciting series. <br/><br/>"My sword flashed, and he screamed as the gun hit the pavement along with both his arms." <br/><br/>Julie starts The Forever Song off with a bang and doesn't let up until it's over. This book is seriously gory!! It's also full of adventure, humor, love, heart-warming moments, and heart-BREAKING moments. <br/><br/>DO NOT READ FURTHER IF YOU HAVEN'T READ THE FIRST TWO BOOKS!!<br/><br/>I have to say, I was VERY concerned for Allison in the beginning of this book. After wh</span>
  <span id="freeText7416649686551448594" style="display:none">Such an epic conclusion to an amazingly exciting series. <br /><br />"My sword flashed, and he screamed as the gun hit the pavement along with both his arms." <br /><br />Julie starts The Forever Song off with a bang and doesn't let up until it's over. This book is seriously gory!! It's also full of adventure, humor, love, heart-warming moments, and heart-BREAKING moments. <br /><br />DO NOT READ FURTHER IF YOU HAVEN'T READ THE FIRST TWO BOOKS!!<br /><br />I have to say, I was VERY concerned for Allison in the beginning of this book. After what happened to Zeke at the end of The Eternity Cure, I just didn't know if she would have the ability to care about anything anymore. She definitely had a couple of Damon (TVD) moments, that's for sure! Humanity switch? Off. The twisted part of me actually kind of liked it, I have to admit, because it led to some seriously sick fight scenes. Seriously. Sick. I can't remember the last time I read a book with the amount of gruesome things as this book had. The faint of heart need not apply. Of course I didn't actually want Allie to stay like this, and at some point we all know she has to come face to face with what's left of Zeke. The question is, WHAT WILL HAPPEN WHEN THEY FINALLY MEET?<br /><br />This stressed me out SO MUCH! And with good reason. Julie does NOT like to make things easy; not for her characters, and certainly not for her readers. I picture her in her room, watching her computer screen while we all read, rubbing her hands together and laughing maniacally at our tormented status updates. MWAHAHAHA! You're cruel, Julie. Just cruel.<br /><br />It isn't all bad times, though. There are so many times when I couldn't stop chuckling at the banter between Allie and Jackal. They seriously were like my two kids. I kept waiting for Kannin to turn around and slap them both upside the head, or put them in a corner until they learned to behave. The character development of Jackal is pretty awesome. If you had tried to tell me, while I read The Immortal Rules, that one day I wouldn't want Allie to decapitate Jackal, burn his body and stick his head on a pike, I would've laughed at you. But that little punk grew on me, and in the end, he had my nerves in a twist just like the rest of them.<br /><br />Oh, and there are other things that happen too....that I can't talk about. But, yeah. Good times. :D<br /><br />Overall, I was really happy with this ending. It was hard, it was heart-breaking, but it was also sadly satisfying, and fitting for this harsh world. I'm so happy that I enjoyed this series from beginning to end, and I can't wait to read what Julie has for us next. (TALON!!)<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7416649686551448594" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1206878991" />
    <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog"><img alt="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576986930p2/28353412.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥" href="/user/show/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog">Jen ♥Star-Crossed Book Blog♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=dont-cry">dont-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=favorite-heroines">favorite-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=go-away-sweaty-palms">go-away-sweaty-palms</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28353412-jen-star-crossed-book-blog?shelf=love-makes-my-heart-happy">love-makes-my-heart-happy</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1206878991" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5357599457561507559"><b>*Spoilers for <a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00ALTVH8O/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=390957&creativeASIN=B00ALTVH8O&linkCode=as2&tag=stacrobooblo-20&linkId=NME5GB7IWCY7FC4X' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Immortal Rules</a><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445611936i/16681607.gif' alt='' width='1' height='1' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> & <a href='http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00FBZL2II/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&camp=1789&creative=390957&creativeASIN=B00FBZL2II&linkCode=as2&tag=stacrobooblo-20&linkId=37Z5QZ5GTBTNITVX' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Eternity Cure</a><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446046752i/16740077.gif' alt='' width='1' height='1' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>*</b><br/><br/><strong>The Forever Song was an epic conclusion to the Blood of Eden trilogy!  It was filled to the brim with devastation, peril, hope, and I cherished every single page.</strong>   Even if I had tears in my eyes through parts of those last few chapters.  But I didn't want it to end since it contained so much of what I loved in the first two books.  Luckily, I know that this series will continue to infiltrate my thoughts for a long time to come.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>Humans meant</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText5357599457561507559" style="display:none"><b>*Spoilers for <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00ALTVH8O/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B00ALTVH8O&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=stacrobooblo-20&amp;linkId=NME5GB7IWCY7FC4X" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Rules</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445611936i/16681607.gif" alt="" width="1" height="1" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> &amp; <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00FBZL2II/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;creativeASIN=B00FBZL2II&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=stacrobooblo-20&amp;linkId=37Z5QZ5GTBTNITVX" rel="nofollow noopener">The Eternity Cure</a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446046752i/16740077.gif" alt="" width="1" height="1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">*</b><br><br><strong>The Forever Song was an epic conclusion to the Blood of Eden trilogy!  It was filled to the brim with devastation, peril, hope, and I cherished every single page.</strong>   Even if I had tears in my eyes through parts of those last few chapters.  But I didn't want it to end since it contained so much of what I loved in the first two books.  Luckily, I know that this series will continue to infiltrate my thoughts for a long time to come.<br><blockquote>
  <b>Humans meant nothing to me, not anymore. They were food, and I was a vampire. I was done pretending that I was anything less than a monster.</b>
  <b>
    <br>
  </b>
  <b>But I </b>
  <b>
    <i>would</i>
  </b>
  <b> kill Sarren.</b>
</blockquote><br><strong>Allie is a broken, dark, devastated mess, and the ties to her humanity have been shredded.</strong>  With the death of Zeke, she can no longer be the same girl she was in the past.  While refusing to mourn, she gets on the road with her brother, Jackal, and her sire, Kanin.  Because while they listened to crazy vamp, aka Sarren, torture Zeke, they heard Zeke give away details to Eden's location.  And with Sarren already on the road headed towards the humans safe haven, they have to hurry.  If he gets there before them, all hell will break loose and no one will be safe.  <strong>But the road to Eden is filled with horrors only Sarren could create.  And none of them contemplated how much </strong><strong><i>more</i> sick and twisted he could get, because they haven't seen anything yet!</strong><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Hey, vampire girl,” Zeke whispered, his voice slightly choked. “I knew...you’d come for me.”</b>
  
    <br>
  
  <b>* * * </b>
  
    <br>
  
  <b>
    <i>This...can’t be real.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><strong>The thing I was the most excited about, because it gave me hope and I <i>need</i></strong><strong> hope,  was that Allie and Zeke had to meet again.  Well, I at least hoped that much was true.  Their love stuck with me because it was pure, dangerous and oh so sweet.</strong>  I fell madly in love with Zeke and I flew through the pages trying to get to him.  But I was scared for their future.   Because do you remember the last line in The Eternity Cure?  I sure couldn't forget it, and it haunted me.  I tried my hardest to figure out what Sarren was up to, and while I got part of it right, I wasn't even close to the other part.  Sarren was the perfect villain and while I appreciate the crazy twists he took this story, I kept hoping he would die a miserable death.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“You are so bloody frustrating!” he roared, back fisting another rabid with the axhead. “Do you really think the cure is worth </b>
  <b>
    <i>this</i>
  </b>
  <b>? You think I’d be here now if that’s all I wanted?” He turned and sliced his weapon through the air, beheading one rabid and sinking it into another. “Get your damn head out of your ass, sister!” he seethed. “And give me a little fucking credit. That’s not why I’m here.” - Jackal</b>
</blockquote><br><strong>But ironically, one of my favorite things about this book was the family aspect between Allie, Jackal and Kanin.</strong>  I started out the series only liking Kanin and loathing Jackal, but while in the midst of this book I found myself caring for both of them.  Deeply.  You see, while Jackal and Allie spent time together in The Eternity Cure, he would make me laugh and smile.  I didn't want to admit it, but I slowly warmed up to him and his charismatic self.  And I loved how him and Kanin treated Allie like family throughout the story.  <strong>Jackal would bicker and pester Allie, as an older brother should,and Kanin was the parent who would threaten or reprimand them to get along.  I can't believe how much their little family made me so happy and warmed my heart.  </strong>But then I wanted to kick myself because now I cared deeply for Jackal and Kanin and I was terrified what their fate could be!<br><blockquote>
  <b>“It is...a very heavy weight to carry, Allison, the damnation of a world. I want you to be very certain, before we go any further. Is it worth it? Is he worth it?” </b>
  
    <br>
  
  <b>His words chilled me, but I already knew my answer. It was selfish, it was unreasonable, and I knew it was the wrong choice. But I looked up at Kanin, into his impassive face, and whispered, “Yes.”</b>
</blockquote><br><strong>I'm so sad to see these characters go, but thankfully each of them got the ending they deserved.  No matter how heartbreaking or happy it made me, I was thrilled with the way the story ended!  </strong>This is the second series I have fallen in love with by Julie Kagawa!  So it's safe to say that yes, <strong>she has become one of my favorite authors.</strong>  And an author that is now on my auto buy list because <strong>her stories are emotional, devastating, heartwarming</strong> and I can't wait to see what all of her future books hold!<br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i> <br><a title="Star-Crossed Book Blog" href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452287496i/17673736._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>

<div id="review_884095260" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/884095260" />
    <a title="Erica Ravenclaw" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12099580-erica-ravenclaw"><img alt="Erica Ravenclaw" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598276462p2/12099580.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/884095260?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erica Ravenclaw" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erica Ravenclaw" href="/user/show/12099580-erica-ravenclaw">Erica Ravenclaw</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20733621-the-forever-song">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12099580-erica-ravenclaw?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer884095260" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5310386046087065890">☆ ☆ ☆ <br/><br/>I'm really going 3.5 here but rounded up because I feel like it. YOU DON'T OWN ME GOODREADS.<br/>EDIT: Changed rating down half a star, it's been a few days and it's just more accurate. <br/><br/><b> No spoilers and colorful language abound! </b><br/><br/>*I received this book in exchange for a review*<br/><br/><a href='http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/anigif_enhanced-8656-1394726651-2_zpse89c0ff5.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395425944ra/8994870.gif' alt=' photo anigif_enhanced-8656-1394726651-2_zpse89c0ff5.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>The Forever Song is a closing chapter on a much loved series Blood of Eden, I was a little late to the party for this author and walked into it blind but boy am I happy to be here. I do not necessarily love the first tw</span>
  <span id="freeText5310386046087065890" style="display:none">☆ ☆ ☆ <br><br>I'm really going 3.5 here but rounded up because I feel like it. YOU DON'T OWN ME GOODREADS.<br>EDIT: Changed rating down half a star, it's been a few days and it's just more accurate. <br><br><b> No spoilers and colorful language abound! </b><br><br>*I received this book in exchange for a review*<br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/anigif_enhanced-8656-1394726651-2_zpse89c0ff5.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395425944ra/8994870.gif" alt=" photo anigif_enhanced-8656-1394726651-2_zpse89c0ff5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>The Forever Song is a closing chapter on a much loved series Blood of Eden, I was a little late to the party for this author and walked into it blind but boy am I happy to be here. I do not necessarily love the first two installments, I do however really enjoy the character development and simply the way that Kagawa writes. Unlike the first two this starts off with Allie fully eclipsed be her deamon, a darkness we have yet to see from her that I fully reveled in. With the monster in control, her sire and her blood brother at her side they set off from New Covington with the singular objective to stop Sarren by any means necessary. <br><br>The road to Eden is is both physically and emotionally tumultuous for our heroine. There are many obstacles Allie must overcome to complete her journey, chief among them learning to accept who she was and who she is now. I have to admit there was a time and a place that I wanted to reach through my kindle screen and shake her bony ass. I was so exasperated by her fucking nonsense that I contemplated throwing in the towel all together. The world was at stake here, the human and vampire race were hanging in the balance and you are going to what? Now? ARE YOU KIDDING?<br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/anigif_enhanced-buzz-22530-1388810195-27_zps96285f07.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395465308ra/9001019.gif" alt=" photo anigif_enhanced-buzz-22530-1388810195-27_zps96285f07.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>...girlwhatthefeckiswrongwithyoustopbeingsostupidihateyou.<br><br>So then, I put myself in a little time out. <br><br><a href="http://s1212.photobucket.com/user/PetiteAme/media/Halloween%20Upload/GIFS/anigif_enhanced-21639-1394980149-8_zps18af1c85.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1395465308ra/9001020.gif" alt=" photo anigif_enhanced-21639-1394980149-8_zps18af1c85.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I decided to beef up my gif library and contemplate if it was worth finishing. I came to terms with the fact that I don't give a hoot about Allie. I thought she was pretty kickass as a human, not so much as a vampire, win some lose some yadda yadda. Jackal and Kanin however were always my favorites and for them I must prevail. For this I give Kagawa credit for all of Sarrens complete utter nonsense, over the top insanity, poetic drivel you have Kanin's stoic, grounded realistic tether into the here and now. For all the immature, wet blanket, self righteous bullshit Allie parades all over the pages, you have Jackal's flippant, in your face, take it or leave it sparkle. The balance was very needed and just as one was getting too ridiculous, the counter would chime and pull it back to the middle. <br><br>As the coven of vampires raced to stop Sarren, Kagawa artfully crafted closure for each of her beloved characters. The end of a series is always one with mixed emotions for both the author and the reader, she remained true to her characters, the characters remained true to themselves. You will have a feast of action, gore, surprises, gut wrenching goodbyes and peaceful resolution. <br><br><br><br><br>BONUS: At the end of The Forever Song we are treated to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/888224853" rel="nofollow noopener"> just a teaser of Talon</a>, and I for one can't wait to read it! <br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://www.ericapetiteame.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395070373i/8942755.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <b>HOW AM I GONNA SURVIVE??!!!</b>

  <span id="freeText6093458275394473301" style="display:none">Lalalaaa, can't wait to read the 3rd book!^^<br>Suddenly.. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384975263ra/7037846.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wait, wait...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386449747ra/7367506.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386449747ra/7367507.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>2014 APRIL 29TH??!!?!???!?!?!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386449747ra/7367508.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386448724ra/7367300.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>Try not to cry.. try not to cry.... <div id="review_2645211986" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2645211986" />
    <a title="Cassie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69117331-cassie"><img alt="Cassie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598972535p2/69117331.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2645211986?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cassie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cassie" href="/user/show/69117331-cassie">Cassie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/34093548-the-forever-song">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69117331-cassie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2645211986" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15169922397742123239"><b> “I love you, vampire girl,” he whispered as he drew back. “And forever is exactly what we have.” </b> <br/><br/>i don’t.... have words. i’m literally sobbing, like full on ugly <br/><b> <u>s o b b i n g. </u></b> <br/><br/>idk what to say. julie kagawa has literally given me hope, made me laugh, and then ripped my heart out and stomped on it, only to return it to me and say, <i> “here, put this thing back in your chest and find a way to cope with what’s about to come next.” </i><br/><br/>my biggest fear in the <u> entire trilogy </u> came true. and it broke so</span>
  <span id="freeText15169922397742123239" style="display:none"><b> “I love you, vampire girl,” he whispered as he drew back. “And forever is exactly what we have.” </b> <br /><br />i don’t.... have words. i’m literally sobbing, like full on ugly <br /><b> <u>s o b b i n g. </u></b> <br /><br />idk what to say. julie kagawa has literally given me hope, made me laugh, and then ripped my heart out and stomped on it, only to return it to me and say, <i> “here, put this thing back in your chest and find a way to cope with what’s about to come next.” </i><br /><br />my biggest fear in the <u> entire trilogy </u> came true. and it broke something in me fierce. i don’t care if these are just fictional characters, okay? i grew to love some of these characters with everything in me. i constantly thought about them some days. and after finishing this third and final book, i will think about them until the end of time. <br /><br />i highly recommend the <i> blood of eden trilogy. </i> it’s got everything a book should have. amazing characters, a great plot, heartbreaking moments, moments you want to savor for the rest of your life, scenes that will make you mad, but will make you have hope at the same time, times where you’ll want to scream, and then laugh two seconds later... you get the point. <br /><br />it took me forever to finish this book, not because it was bad, <b> oh no. but because i didn’t want to say goodbye to this world or these characters. and now that i have? i truly left a piece of my soul with this book when i read that last sentence. </b> <br /><br />so, please, do yourselves a favor and treat yourself to this wonderfully devastating world that julie has created. you won’t regret it, trust me.<br /><br /><i> “I hope I’m doing what you wanted, what you tried to teach me. It’s going to take a long time, but I won’t give up, just like you didn’t give up. And I pray that, wherever you are, you’ve finally found your peace.” </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="15169922397742123239" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1384448629" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1384448629" />
    <a title="Kira Simion" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27960680-kira-simion"><img alt="Kira Simion" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528008824p2/27960680.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1384448629?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kira Simion" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kira Simion" href="/user/show/27960680-kira-simion">Kira Simion</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27960680-kira-simion?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1384448629" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3760862126020628691">Guess who just got this book <del> from the library </del>? :D<br/><br/>*points* This gal! <b>*Tears of joy*</b><br/><br/><i> Please let Jackal not die. And please let them both kick some butt! </i> *^* *crosses fingers*<br/><br/>The first book was good, the second was really great, so I have some hope for the third one. :3<br/><br/><b> Edit: </b> (To be reviewed as best I can)<br/><br/><b> Edit: (7-7-16) </b> (btw you need to read these books in order. There are some series that can be read out of order but, this is not one of them.)<br/><br/>I don't know how to explain how great this trilog</span>
  <span id="freeText3760862126020628691" style="display:none">Guess who just got this book <del> from the library </del>? :D<br /><br />*points* This gal! <b>*Tears of joy*</b><br /><br /><i> Please let Jackal not die. And please let them both kick some butt! </i> *^* *crosses fingers*<br /><br />The first book was good, the second was really great, so I have some hope for the third one. :3<br /><br /><b> Edit: </b> (To be reviewed as best I can)<br /><br /><b> Edit: (7-7-16) </b> (btw you need to read these books in order. There are some series that can be read out of order but, this is not one of them.)<br /><br />I don't know how to explain how great this trilogy truly was. I really don't. (I lack the expertise of words. :() (I'll try though.)<br /><br />So let's start with the characters. Wow. From the first book to the third you can see the immense development in the main character and I defiantly ADORED that. I felt for the characters, from the smart aleck Jackal with his quips to Kanin with his <del> senpai </del> sensei like behavior. (<b> <del> Teach me master. </del></b>  *^* Even Zeke had his moments when he had to get used to being the new him. (Trying not to spoil hahaha.)<br /><br />The plot was intense and action packed with hunting rabids to trying to kill Sarren, the guy who wants to end the world with a new strain of viruses. The new virus will be stronger than the one that caused some people to turn into rabids. This one causes both vampires and humans to want to rip their eyes out and tear at anything that moves (rabids did this too but, they were easier to destroy and weren't as infectious.)<br /><br />Overall, I really enjoyed this trilogy and hope to read more fantastic books (by this author or another.) :D<br /><br />5/5 stars!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3760862126020628691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5hXsWM9CvNfhn3zYBXbWOoTkW+4bpEthi/apOLn9vz9misbUx3BW59NTE+kElntS8vhIL1dO1moSJMqVBJPm/w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pw8sZk6XQ6+3JQUaY7hPfm0UZ9KNTsq23iM2CexNjyUnkAbqRqWpn4XpaitiWOIWGwh0E8GkV71H8VWkUSPW5Q==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
